	<script>
		AE.defer(function(){
		var dot=new AE.widget.beacondot({
			containerID: 'relatedSearchContainer',
			data:{
				mt_sepd_sek : encodeURIComponent("121303"),
				mt_pos : "10105",
				mt_logic : "1"
			}
		});
		dot.start();
	});
	function displayBoxItem(isViewAll){
		var boxContainerId  = 'relatedSearchContainer';
		var boxStyleClass   = 'clearfix';
		var buttonMoreId    = 'btnViewMore';
		var buttonLessId    = 'btnViewLess';
		
		var boxContainer = YAHOO.util.Dom.get(boxContainerId);
		var buttonMore   = YAHOO.util.Dom.get(buttonMoreId);
		var buttonLess   = YAHOO.util.Dom.get(buttonLessId);
		var searchBoxs   = YAHOO.util.Dom.getChildrenBy(boxContainer, function(el){return YAHOO.util.Dom.hasClass(el, boxStyleClass);});
		if(searchBoxs.length <= 1){
			YAHOO.util.Dom.setStyle([buttonMore, buttonLess], 'display', 'none');
		} else {
			if(isViewAll){
				YAHOO.util.Dom.setStyle(searchBoxs, 'display', '');
				YAHOO.util.Dom.setStyle(buttonLess, 'display', '');
				YAHOO.util.Dom.setStyle(buttonMore, 'display', 'none');
			}else{
				searchBoxs.shift();
				YAHOO.util.Dom.setStyle(searchBoxs, 'display', 'none');
				YAHOO.util.Dom.setStyle(buttonLess, 'display', 'none');
				YAHOO.util.Dom.setStyle(buttonMore, 'display', '');
			}
		}
	}
	displayBoxItem(false);
</script>
